+ "searchutil -c analytics:heartbeat:index:<shorthand>  : dump live per-index heartbeat fields for the given index.\n"
+ "searchutil -c analytics:heartbeat:read    : load heartbeat.plist from disk into memory. WARNING: overwrites any in-memory accumulations not yet written to disk. Use 'send' for live state.\n"
+ "searchutil -c analytics:heartbeat:reset   : reset all accumulated heartbeat counters to 0, as if a heartbeat was just sent. Re-arms any in-progress throttle episode to the current timestamp.\n"
+ "searchutil -c analytics:heartbeat:send    : snapshot live index stats and send a com.apple.spotlight.heartbeat CA event. Does NOT reset counters (use 'reset' explicitly). Safe to call repeatedly.\n"
+ "searchutil -c analytics:heartbeat:shared  : refresh and dump only the shared (non-per-index) heartbeat fields.\n"
+ "searchutil -c analytics:heartbeat:write   : flush current in-memory heartbeat data to heartbeat.plist without resetting.\n"
+ "searchutil -c analytics:index:<shorthand>  : dump raw analyticsCreationData and analyticsCountData for the given index (from disk, not live).\n"
+ "searchutil -c analytics:indexdrop:last  : dump the contents of the most recently modified index drop report.\n"
+ "searchutil -c analytics:indexdrop:list  : list all index drop report filenames on disk (all time).\n"
+ "searchutil -c analytics:inject:memory:0   : record a memory-pressure-normal transition in analytics (analytics-only).\n"
+ "searchutil -c analytics:inject:memory:1   : record a memory-pressure-critical transition in analytics (analytics-only; does NOT call si_flushCaches or set gMemoryPressureCritical).\n"
+ "searchutil -c analytics:inject:queue:<shorthand>  : increment count_queue_pressure by 1 for the given index. Use with 'heartbeat:send' to verify the counter is wired.\n"
+ "searchutil -c analytics:inject:thermal:0  : set gSIBadThermals=NO — restores normal thread count and closes the in-progress throttle episode.\n"
+ "searchutil -c analytics:inject:thermal:1  : set gSIBadThermals=YES — limits indexing threads and fires count_thermal_throttle telemetry. Mirrors the real thermal notification path.\n"

If a destination is not specified, reports will be copied over to the ~/Library/Logs/CrashReporter/DiagnosticLogs/Search directory.\n"

- "searchutil -c analytics:heartbeat:index:<shorthand>  : collect and dump values of per-index heartbeat fields.\n"
- "searchutil -c analytics:heartbeat:read  : read heartbeat.plist into memory; note that this might undo any in-memory updates.\n"
- "searchutil -c analytics:heartbeat:reset  : reset certain fields as if a Spotlight heartbeat event has been reported.\n"
- "searchutil -c analytics:heartbeat:send  : create Spotlight heartbeat event and send it to CoreAnalytics.\n"
- "searchutil -c analytics:heartbeat:shared  : refresh shared heartbeat fields and dump values.\n"
- "searchutil -c analytics:heartbeat:write  : flush out in-memory heartbeat data to heartbeat.plist\n"
- "searchutil -c analytics:index:<shorthand>  : dump contents of index's analyticsCreationData and analyticsCountData files.\n"
